Ole Miss QB Jordan Ta'amu had 76 yards rushing on 13 carries in the first half.  In the second half, Ta'amu had -10 yards on 8 carries. #Gamecocks
Josh Vann had 3 catches for 13 yards and 1 TD.  The TD reception was the first of his career. #Gamecocks
Bryan Edwards had 4 receptions for 109 yards and 1 TD.  The 75 yard reception is a career long.  His longest reception prior to yesterday was the 73 yarder against Tennessee on October 27, 2018.  He has 4 career 100-yard receiving games. #Gamecocks
Ty'Son Williams had 3 receptions for 105 yards.  Both are career highs.  His previous career highs were 2 receptions and 16 yards receiving. #Gamecocks
Jake Bentley's rushing touchdown was his first of the season.  Bentley scored 6 rushing touchdowns in 2017. #Gamecocks
Mon Denson ran for a career high 102 yards.  His previous career high was 61 against Florida last season.  Denson entered Saturday's game with a season total of 66 rushing yards. #Gamecocks
Some 4th quarter stats.  Ole Miss had 18 yards on 19 plays.  The #Gamecocks had 111 yards on 21 plays.  85 of Carolina's 111 yards came on the ground. The Rebels ran for 8 yards and passed for 10.
Ole Miss was 5-9 on third down in the first half.  The Rebels went 1-8 in the second half. #Gamecocks
Deebo Samuel's KOR for a TD was the 4th of his career.  His last KOR for a TD was on September 9, 2017 at Missouri. #Gamecocks
